## Ancient North history ##
## By HobbesMkII ##
##Fire and Blood Update and later maintenance by Paxter Redwyne and Alex "Kuczaja" Kwiatek##

###Ancient Stark History
###In Colaboration with Chrisjm89 knuckey
###Added some non-canon Starks between King Walton and King Edwyn, if any new info will be revealed by Martin about this time period it can be removed###Paxter Redwyne
###Added three new lords of winterfell, Brandon the Boisterous (son of King Torrhen), Roderick Stark (son of Brandon the Boisterous) and Brandon the Boastful (son of Roderick and father of Walton and Alaric)
###I've also added two other sons of Brandon the Boisterous, Harrion, who Lynara Stark (Cregan Stark's third wife) comes from and Rickard, a third son since Harrion is said to be a younger son instead of the youngest
821059 = {
	name = "Брандон" # Brandon the Builder
	dynasty = 59

	martial = 12

	diplomacy = 15

		birth = yes
		create_bloodline = {
			type = bran_the_builder
			has_dlc = "Holy Fury"
		}
	}
	110.1.1 = { death = yes }
}
